gcc -g -std=c17 -Wall -o compiler `cat sources.txt`
DIFFS=0; \
for f in `echo hw4-vmtest*.pl0 | sed -e 's/\\.pl0//g'`; \
do \
	echo compiling "$f.pl0" ...; \
	rm -f "$f.myvi"; \
	./compiler "$f.pl0" > "$f.myvi"; \
	echo running "$f.myvi" in the VM ...; \
	vm/vm "$f.myvi" > "$f.myvo" 2>&1; \
	diff -w -B "$f.vmo" "$f.myvo" && echo 'passed!' \
		|| { echo 'failed!'; DIFFS=1; }; \
done; \
if test 0 = $DIFFS; \
then \
	echo 'All tests passed!'; \
else \
	echo 'Test(s) failed!'; \
fi
